 1

 1
 In case of breathlessness, if someone is lying in unconscious state in front of you and does not respond even after repeated calls or shaking hands, then immediately lie on the ground on the ground
 check karen ki uski saanse chal raheen he yaa nahin
 Turn your head and apply pressure on the chest and rub fast

 2

 4

 1

 us samay srilanka kaa score 70 ran par do wicket tha or thirimane 27 ran ke nijee score par ballebaaji kar rahe the

 unhone 37 gendon kaa saamana kar teen chauke or ek chakka lagaaya

 saaha kaa bhi wicket perera ne liya

 saaha ne ampire ke faisle ke khilaaf diares liya tha lekin tivi ampire wilson ne use nakaar diya

 bhubaneshwar kumaar (13) kaa wicket 146 ke score par gira

 bhuvi ko suranga lackmal ne out kiya

 donon ne kai joardaar shots lagaae

 shami ne 22 gendon kaa saamana kiya

 ''samir saxena,web series creatre*** Meeting the five-decade-old demand of the people of Telangana region, the United Progressive Alliance (UPA) government on Tuesday decided to split Andhra Pradesh and allow Telangana to be made a separate state
 samprag ke is nirnay se telugubhashi logon ke liye do rajya ban jaaenge
 The upa's coordination committee approved the formation of a separate Telangana state in New Delhi
 pradhanmantri ke nivas par mangalvaar ko hui baithak ke baad naagarik uddyan mantri ajit singh ne kaha, "sabhi dalon ne sarvasammati se telugana ke paksh main nirnay liya he
 " baithak main congress, rashtravaadi congress party (rakanpa), neshnal conference or rashtriya lokdal (ralod) ke netaaon ne hissaa liya
 After the upa's coordination committee meeting, the Congress Working Committee (CWC) also passed a resolution requesting the central government to split Andhra Pradesh and form a separate Telangana state
 pruthak telugana ke gathan kii maang vaale prastaav main seedblusi ne kaha he ki agle 10 varsh ke liye hyderabad ko andhra pradesh or telugana kii sanyukt rajdhani rahane diya jaae
 After the CWC meeting, Congress spokesperson Ajay Maken said that the meeting of the CWC was chaired by party president Sonia Gandhi and the meeting was also attended by Prime Minister Manmohan Singh and Congress vice-president Rahul Gandhi
 maakan ne paarit prastaav padhakar bataaya, "centre sarkaar se yah anurodh prastaavit he ki vah pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan ke liye kadam uthaae
 " kendriya maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantri em
 M
 pallam raju ne isse pehle sanket diya tha ki congress ke netaa pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan kaa nirnay lene ke paksh main hai
 The issue of Andhra Pradesh and Telangana (then Hyderabad State), which was formed on November 1, 1956, after the formation of the state of Andhra Pradesh, was sealed with this decision of the UPA
 bhashik aadhaar par gathit andhra pradesh desh kaa aisa pehla rajya hoga jiskaa vibhaajan hoga
 After the formation of the state, the area of telangana was 1
 14 lakh varg kilometre hoga tathaa isaki aabaadi 35
 38 crores
 andhra pradesh kii 294 vidhansabha siton main se 117 vidhansabha seat telugana main hai, tathaa telugana kshetra se loksabhaa main 17 saansad hai
 In 1969, more than 300 people were killed in police firing, mostly involving young students, in the 'jai Telangana' movement to make Telangana a separate state
 pruthak telugana ke gathan ke liye centre sarkaar ne 2009 se sakriy prayaas shuru kiye or is dauraan kisi thos nirnay par na pahunch paane ke kaaran sattarudh samprag sarkaar kii sabase badi party congress ko rajya ke chunaav main kaaphi nuksaan uthaanaa padaa
 Many Congress mps in the state joined the Telangana Rashtra Samithi (TRS), a party fighting for Telangana
 tiares or anya dalon ne centre sarkaar par pruthak telugana rajya gathit kiye jane ke liye lagaataar dabaav banaae rakhaa
 Last month, two Congress mps and senior leaders K
K
 keshav raav ke is mudde par congress se istipha dene ke saath hi congress par is par koi thos nirnay lene kaa dabaav or bad gaya
 Finally, the Congress, the largest constituent of the UPA, called a meeting on Tuesday to resolve the issue unanimously before the general elections due next year, in which the formation of a separate Telangana state was unanimously approved
 samprag kii samanvay samiti main hissaa lene ke liye mangalvaar ko simandhra or telugana se anek netaa dilli pahunche
 Many mps including Union ministers from Seemandhra and many ministers of the state came to Delhi with the aim of stopping the partition of the state

 baithak main congress, rashtravaadi congress party (rakanpa), neshnal conference or rashtriya lokdal (ralod) ke netaaon ne hissaa liya
 After the upa's coordination committee meeting, the Congress Working Committee (CWC) also passed a resolution requesting the central government to split Andhra Pradesh and form a separate Telangana state
 pruthak telugana ke gathan kii maang vaale prastaav main seedblusi ne kaha he ki agle 10 varsh ke liye hyderabad ko andhra pradesh or telugana kii sanyukt rajdhani rahane diya jaae
 After the CWC meeting, Congress spokesperson Ajay Maken said that the meeting of the CWC was chaired by party president Sonia Gandhi and the meeting was also attended by Prime Minister Manmohan Singh and Congress vice-president Rahul Gandhi
 maakan ne paarit prastaav padhakar bataaya, "centre sarkaar se yah anurodh prastaavit he ki vah pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan ke liye kadam uthaae
 " kendriya maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantri em

 pallam raju ne isse pehle sanket diya tha ki congress ke netaa pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan kaa nirnay lene ke paksh main hai
 The issue of Andhra Pradesh and Telangana (then Hyderabad State), which was formed on November 1, 1956, after the formation of the state of Andhra Pradesh, was sealed with this decision of the UPA
 bhashik aadhaar par gathit andhra pradesh desh kaa aisa pehla rajya hoga jiskaa vibhaajan hoga
 After the formation of the state, the area of telangana was 1
 14 lakh varg kilometre hoga tathaa isaki aabaadi 35
 38 crores
 andhra pradesh kii 294 vidhansabha siton main se 117 vidhansabha seat telugana main hai, tathaa telugana kshetra se loksabhaa main 17 saansad hai
 In 1969, more than 300 people were killed in police firing, mostly involving young students, in the 'jai Telangana' movement to make Telangana a separate state
 pruthak telugana ke gathan ke liye centre sarkaar ne 2009 se sakriy prayaas shuru kiye or is dauraan kisi thos nirnay par na pahunch paane ke kaaran sattarudh samprag sarkaar kii sabase badi party congress ko rajya ke chunaav main kaaphi nuksaan uthaanaa padaa
 Many Congress mps in the state joined the Telangana Rashtra Samithi (TRS), a party fighting for Telangana
 tiares or anya dalon ne centre sarkaar par pruthak telugana rajya gathit kiye jane ke liye lagaataar dabaav banaae rakhaa

K
 keshav raav ke is mudde par congress se istipha dene ke saath hi congress par is par koi thos nirnay lene kaa dabaav or bad gaya
 Finally, the Congress, the largest constituent of the UPA, called a meeting on Tuesday to resolve the issue unanimously before the general elections due next year, in which the formation of a separate Telangana state was unanimously approved
 samprag kii samanvay samiti main hissaa lene ke liye mangalvaar ko simandhra or telugana se anek netaa dilli pahunche
 Many mps including Union ministers from Seemandhra and many ministers of the state came to Delhi with the aim of stopping the partition of the state
 telugana ke netaaon ne ek pruthak baithak ke baad vishwaas vyakt kiya ki congress kshetra ke logon ke itane lambey samay se chale aa rahe sapane ko saakaar karegi

 Some Congress mps from Andhra Pradesh are also opposing the formation of a separate Telangana state, and in this regard last week they had also met the Prime Minister and demanded not to divide the state
 samprag kii samanvay samiti kii baithak ke baad congress kaary samiti (seedblusi) ne bhi ek prastaav paarit kar centre sarkaar se andhra pradesh ko vibhajit kar pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan kaa anurodh kiya
 In the proposal seeking the creation of a separate Telangana, the CWC has said that Hyderabad should be allowed to be the joint capital of Andhra Pradesh and Telangana for the next 10 years
 seedblusi kii baithak ke baad congress ke pravaktaa ajay maakan ne kaha ki seedblusi kii baithak kii adhyakshata party kaa adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne kii tathaa baithak main pradhanmantri manmohan singh or congress ke upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ne bhi hissaa liya

 Pallam Raju had earlier indicated that Congress leaders were in favor of deciding to form a separate Telangana state
 andhra state or telugana (tab kaa hyderabad state) ko milakar ek november 1956 ko gathit kiye gaye rajya andhra pradesh ke gathan ke baad se hi chale aa rahe is mudde kaa samprag ke is nirnay ke saath hi patakshep ho gaya
 Andhra Pradesh, formed on a linguistic basis, will be the first state in the country to be partitioned
 rajya banane ke baad telugana kaa kshetrafal 1
 It will be 14 lakh square kilometers and its population will be 35
 38 karod hogi
 Of the 294 assembly seats in Andhra Pradesh, 117 assembly seats are in Telangana, and there are 17 mps in the Lok Sabha from the Telangana region
 telugana ko alag rajya banane ke liye 'jai telugana' andolan main 1969 main 300 se adhik logon kii police golibari main maut ho gai thi, jisamen adhiktar yuva chaatr shaamil the
 The central government started active efforts to form a separate Telangana from 2009 and during this time the Congress, the largest party in the ruling UPA government, suffered a lot in the state elections due to not reaching any concrete decision
 rajya main congress ke anek saansad telugana ke liye sangharsh kar rahi party telugana raashtra samiti (tiares) main shaamil ho gaye
 The TRS and other parties continued to pressurize the central government to constitute a separate Telangana state
 pichley maheene congress ke do saasandon or varisht netaa ke
 With Keshav Rao's resignation from the Congress on this issue, the pressure on the Congress to take a firm decision on it further increased
 antat: samprag ke sabase bade ghatak dal congress ne agle varsh hone vaale aam chunaav se pehle sarvasammati se is mudde ko sulajhane ke liye mangalvaar ko baithak bulaai, jisamen pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan ko sarvasammati se sweekruti de di gai
 Several leaders from Seemandhra and Telangana reached Delhi on Tuesday to participate in the upa's coordination committee
 simandhra se kendriya mantriyon sahit kai saansad evam rajya ke anek mantri rajya ke vibhaajan ko rokane ke uddeshy se dilli aae the
 Telangana leaders expressed confidence after a separate meeting that the Congress would realize the long-cherished dream of the people of the region
